- fourth element, the frequency of the word scored ranging from 1 for rarely used to 10 for very commonly used.

- fourth element, the frequency of the word scored ranging from 1 for rarely used to 10 for very commonly used.
adjectives
return only the list of the lists in python format. Use double quote for elements of list.
